 In Delhi, the Aam Aadmi Party has engaged in encircling the BJP from the Parliament to the road with regard to ceiling
 is bich ceiling or epadiai ke khilaaf patel chowk se sansad tak virodh march karne pahunche kaaryakartao par police ne jamkar lathi charge kiya
 Aam Aadmi Party workers had gathered at Patel Chowk metro station at 10 am on Monday
 party ke vidhayak, parshad or alag-alag vidhansabha se aae samarthakon ne kareeb 2 ghante tak patel chowk par narebaaji kii
 The BJP was surrounded by posters and banners during the protest
 pradarshnakariyon ne sadak par baithkar dharna diya or gaanaa gaate hue ceiling or epadiai kaa virodh kiya
 During the protest, the common men of the party were seen protesting with a basket of pakoras
 pakora lekar virodh kar rahe pradarshnkaree raaj garg ne kaha ki notebandi, jiesti or ceiling karakar modi sarkaar vyapriyon kaa shoshan kar rahi he
 We demand that the central government bring an ordinance in Parliament to get rid of ceiling
 aam aadmi party ke virodh pradarshan ke liye police ne suraksha kaa baari bandobast kiya tha
 At Patel Chowk, barricades and police personnel blocked the road with ropes
 kuch hi der main 'aap' samarthak achaanak sansad kii taraf teji se badhane lage or thodi duuri maujuud police daste se pradarshnakariyon kii dhakka mukki hone lagi
 Meanwhile, the police charged lathi, after which chaos broke out at Patel Chowk
 udhar aam aadmi party ke netaaon kaa kahana he ki pradarshan shanti purv tareeke se kiya ja rahaa tha iske baavjood police ne dandon se kaaryakartaaon ko peeta
 The AAP alleges that the dictatorial government of the BJP has no regard for the businessmen
 aam aadmi partike virodh ko bijepi police ke bal par dabaanaa chaahati he
 Feeling the call for an early election, the BJP, in an effort to bring more and more parties into its fold and expand its sphere of influence, allay fears of allies against secularism and any sense of discrimination or injustice towards minorities
 Tried to assure not to be
 is maheene kii 26 taarikh se shuru hui bijepi kii ek-divasiy kaaryakarini or do-divasiy rashtriya parishad kii baithak main vichaar manthan ke baad shuukravaar ko samaapan sandesh main party ke sheersh netaa laalkrishna adwani ne aagaah kiya, hamen apane bade sahyogi dalon ko pun: aashwaasan dena hoga ki unhen bijepi ke saath sahyog karne ke bare main kisi prakaar kii koi ashanka nahin honi chahie
 For this, our commitment to secularism needs to be reintroduced in such a way that their apprehensions are proved to be unmindful
 kattar hindutv ke chehre gujarat ke mukhyamantri narendra modi ko pradhanmantri pad kaa ummidavaar banaae jane kii sambhaavnaaon par sahyogi dal jediu kii kadi mukhafalat ke bich adwani ke is bayaan ko mahatvapurn mana ja rahaa he
 Indicating the strategy of expanding the party's sphere of influence, Advani also said that we should strongly reassure our brothers in the minority community that there is no discrimination or any sense of injustice in the party's views
 Is not
